# Mews Booking Engine Guide | Booking Engine Guide

Welcome to the online documentation for the **Mews Booking Engine**. We're here to guide you through the process of integrating the Mews Booking Engine into your website, so your guests can create reservations in your properties directly in **Mews Operations**. You can do this in one of three ways:

*   [Booking Engine Standalone](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-standalone)
     Redirect to a standalone booking page hosted by Mews
    
*   [Booking Engine Widget](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-widget)
     Embed a JavaScript widget into your own website
    
*   [Booking Engine API](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api)
     Create your own custom booking engine using the Booking Engine API
    

Not sure which option is right for you? See [Ways to integrate](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/faq/ways-to-integrate)
. If you need further assistance, or have any questions or special requests, please open a ticket from Mews Operations via our Mews Digital Assistant.

> #### 
> 
> [](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide#terminology)
> 
> Terminology
> 
> You may see reference to the term _Distributor_, either in the Guide, in URLs or in code snippets, this is the old name for the _Mews Booking Engine_ before it was re-branded. So if you see _Distributor_, this is synonymous with _Mews Booking Engine_. For a full description of all the terms used in the Guide, see the [Mews Glossary for Open API users](https://help.mews.com/s/article/Mews-Glossary-for-Open-API-users?language=en_US)
> .

> #### 
> 
> [](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide#changes-to-this-guide)
> 
> Changes to this Guide
> 
> *   For the history of changes to the Guide, see the [Changelog](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/changelog)
>     
> *   For important information on deprecations in the API, see [Deprecations](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/deprecations)
>     
> *   To track changes and updates to any part of the Guide, you can follow the [GitHub repository](https://github.com/MewsSystems/gitbook-booking-engine/tree/master)
>     

[NextBooking Engine Standalone](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-standalone)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Booking Engine Standalone | Booking Engine Guide

Booking Engine Standalone is a version of the Booking Engine hosted by Mews. It's the simplest way to connect your website with a booking engine, enabling your guests to make direct bookings in your properties. This section describes how to use it.

# FAQ | Booking Engine Guide

Here we address some Frequently Asked Questions concerning the Mews Booking Engine integration.

*   [Which method should I use to integrate?](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/faq#which-method-should-i-use-to-integrate)
    
*   [Where can I get Configuration ID?](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/faq#where-can-i-get-configuration-id)
    
*   [Why doesn't the Booking Engine use the Configuration IDs I've provided?](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/faq#why-doesnt-the-booking-engine-use-the-configuration-ids-ive-provided)
    
*   [Where can I get City ID?](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/faq#where-can-i-get-city-id)
    
*   [Where can I get Age Category ID?](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/faq#where-can-i-get-age-category-id)
    

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/faq#which-method-should-i-use-to-integrate)

Which method should I use to integrate?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

See [Ways to integrate](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/faq/ways-to-integrate)
.

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/faq#where-can-i-get-configuration-id)

Where can I get Configuration ID?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Booking Engine Configuration ID is a unique identifier for your particular Booking Engine implementation. You can find it in **Mews Operations**.

*   Start on the **Dashboard** (the main screen).
    
*   In the left-hand menu, select **Settings** -> **Services**.
    
*   In the section **Bookable services**, select the service which has the Booking Engine configuration. If there's just one service, select that one.
    
*   On the left, select **Booking engines**.
    
*   Select the configuration you want to use.
    
*   In the upper section there is a field **Identifier**. This is your Configuration ID. It has the format `aaaaaaaa-bbbb-cccc-dddd-eeeeeeeeeeee`.
    

![](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3292240558-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtIc30XOAP46ahd8X73va%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-81c9875a1f24a7148ab82076b5214d5acbada394%252Fcommander-configuration-id.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2d5eff0b&sv=2)

Configuration ID in Mews Operations

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/faq#why-doesnt-the-booking-engine-use-the-configuration-ids-ive-provided)

Why doesn't the Booking Engine use the Configuration IDs I've provided?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If the Booking Engine is not using the Configuration IDs provided, it could be that some of those IDs are not valid Configuration IDs. Please check that:

*   All used Configuration IDs are really Configuration IDs, not chain, enterprise or other IDs
    
*   All used Configuration IDs are defined in **Mews Operations** from the same [environment](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/guidelines/environments)
     as the Booking Engine you are using.
    
*   You are using only one Configuration ID per enterprise.
    

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/faq#where-can-i-get-city-id)

Where can I get City ID?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can find the Mews City ID in **Mews Operations**:

*   Start on the **Dashboard** (the main screen).
    
*   In the left-hand menu, select **Settings** -> **Services**.
    
*   In the section **Bookable services**, select the service which has the Booking Engine configuration. If there's just one service, select that one.
    
*   On the left, select **Booking engines**.
    
*   Select the configuration you want to use.
    
*   In the upper section there ia a field **City Identifier**. This is your City ID. It has a format `aaaaaaaa-bbbb-cccc-dddd-eeeeeeeeeeee`.
    

![](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3292240558-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtIc30XOAP46ahd8X73va%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-1968fcc9e08bbfffb38f7e719cde1d1293054e05%252Fcommander-city-id.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d47e8b22&sv=2)

City ID in Mews Operations

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/faq#where-can-i-get-age-category-id)

Where can I get Age Category ID?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can find the AgeCategory ID in **Mews Operations**:

*   Start on the **Dashboard** (the main screen).
    
*   In the left-hand menu, select **Settings** -> **Services**.
    
*   In the section **Bookable services**, select the service which has the Booking Engine configuration. If there's just one service, select that one.
    
*   On the left, select **Age categories**.
    
*   Select the age category you want.
    
*   In the URL there is an ID at the end, right after `/Detail/`. This is the age category ID. It has the format `aaaaaaaa-bbbb-cccc-dddd-eeeeeeeeeeee`.
    

![](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fgithub.com%2FMewsSystems%2Fgitbook-booking-engine%2Fassets%2F22661032%2F8d69a7ad-d641-4021-b9f1-788c9bb07df0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=446619ac&sv=2)

ageCategoryId

# Deprecations | Booking Engine Guide

Deprecations are features of the API which you are discouraged from using, even though they may still be supported for a period of time for the sake of backwards compatibility. Such features are normally deprecated because they are superseded by a better alternative. They can include object properties or entire API operations. The list of deprecations is as follows. Individual items are also highlighted in the [Changelog](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/changelog)
 when they occur. Historic deprecations that have already been discontinued may not be listed.

**For more information, see our** [**Deprecations Policy**](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/open-api/staying-up-to-date/deprecations-policy)
**.**

> **Important:** We strongly advise you to review this list and if you are using any of the deprecated items in your integration, to update your implementation accordingly.

The table columns have the following meanings:

*   **Object** - JSON data object containing the deprecated field or property
    
*   **Property** - Field or property which is deprecated
    
*   **Replaced by** - What the replacement is, if applicable
    
*   **Context** - The context in which the property is used, usually the API operation
    
*   **Deprecated** - The date at which the deprecation notice was given (see the [Changelog](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/changelog)
    )
    
*   **Discontinued** - The date at which it is planned to discontinue the feature completely; a value of '-' indicates no date has been set
    

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/deprecations#deprecated-object-properties)

Deprecated object properties


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Object

Property

Replaced by

Context

Deprecated

Discontinued

# Integrations | Booking Engine Guide

The Booking Engine Widget supports direct integration with [Google Tag Manager](https://marketingplatform.google.com/about/tag-manager/)
 and [Google Analytics](https://marketingplatform.google.com/about/analytics/)
. The integration with Google Tag Manager is intended only to serve data to Google Analytics.

> #### 
> 
> [](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/integrations#disclaimer-regarding-google-analytics-data-accuracy)
> 
> 🚨 Disclaimer regarding Google Analytics data accuracy
> 
> We understand that some property owners have expressed concerns about discrepancies between the data they see in Google Analytics (GA) and the actual reality. It’s essential to be aware of the following factors:
> 
> **Ad Blockers impact**
> 
> *   Approximately 33% of internet users utilize ad blockers, which can block Google Analytics and Google Tag Manager (GTM) scripts. See for example this article for a reference: [https://backlinko.com/ad-blockers-users](https://backlinko.com/ad-blockers-users)
>     .
>     
> *   Consequently, the data received from these services may not be 100% accurate.
>     
> *   Metrics such as revenue and the number of bookings may appear lower than the actual figures, due to ad-blocking behavior.
>     
> 
> **Consent and tracking**
> 
> *   If a guest declines cookies or tracking, their interactions won’t be tracked in Google Analytics.
>     
> 
> Please remember to address these considerations when interpreting GA data and making business decisions.

*   [Google Tag Manager](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/integrations/google-tag-manager)
    
*   [Google Triggers Reference](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/integrations/google-triggers-reference)
    
*   [Google Tag Manager - Configuration](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/integrations/gtm-skeleton)
    
*   [Google Analytics cross-domain tracking](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/integrations/ga-cross-domain-tracking)
    

[PreviousDeprecations](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/deprecations)
[NextGoogle Tag Manager](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/integrations/google-tag-manager)

Last updated 1 year ago

Was this helpful?

# Troubleshooting | Booking Engine Guide

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-widget/troubleshooting#booking-engine-shows-an-error-api.mews.com-refused-to-connect)

Booking Engine shows an error "api.mews.com refused to connect"


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-widget/troubleshooting#fault-description)

Fault description

The browser says it can't open the page because of security, or there's a console error mentioning `api.mews.com` and `X-Frame-Options`.

**Example 1 (Chrome browser):**

![](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3292240558-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtIc30XOAP46ahd8X73va%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-108fe5738d60aa9da9dc3705be53c575ed871b77%252Fapi-mews-com-refused-connect-chrome.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8da369e5&sv=2)

api.mews.com refused error Google Chrome

**Example 2 (Firefox browser):**

![](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3292240558-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtIc30XOAP46ahd8X73va%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-a0fa6318ecedf3ba38f58ad414b78837d2754f8a%252Fapi-mews-com-refused-connect-firefox.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2f13b3d1&sv=2)

api.mews.com refused error Mozilla Firefox

**Example 3 (Console errors):**

*   `[Error] Refused to display 'https://api.mews.com/distributor' in a frame because it set 'X-Frame-Options' to 'sameorigin'.`
    
*   `The loading of "https://api.mews.com/distributor" in a frame is denied by "X-Frame-Options" directive set to "sameorigin".`
    

### 

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-widget/troubleshooting#fault-explanation)

Fault explanation

The Booking Engine Widget is not working because it is not installed correctly on your page. Installing the Booking Engine Widget in any other way than as described in this Guide is not supported and can cause errors such as "api.mews.com refused to connect".

You can try to confirm the Booking Engine Widget is not installed correctly by inspecting the DOM of the page, as follows:

*   Open the page with the Booking Engine Widget and make it show the error
    
*   Open your browser developer tools with 'DOM/elements inspector'
    
*   In the inspector, look for any tags like `<iframe src="https://api.mews.com/distributor/aaaaaaaa-bbbb-cccc-dddd-eeeeeeeeeeee">`
    
*   There shouldn't be any iframe tag with a `src` attribute pointing to the `api.mews.com` domain. If you find something like that, the problem could be in the way the Booking Engine Widget is installed. And even if you didn't find anything like that, it's better to check if the Booking Engine Widget is installed correctly.
    

### 

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-widget/troubleshooting#how-to-fix-it)

How to fix it

First decide if you want to use Booking Engine Standalone or Booking Engine Widget (see [Ways to integrate](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/faq/ways-to-integrate)
). Then go through the relevant installation guide and make sure your page and code is doing everything correctly:

*   [Booking Engine Standalone - Getting started guide](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-standalone/getting-started)
    
*   [Booking Engine Widget - Getting started guide](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-widget/getting-started)
    

If you are using the Booking Engine Widget, pay special attention to the [Requirements](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-widget/getting-started#requirements)
 section of the Booking Engine Widget Getting started guide, it has a list of things to do and a list of common mistakes that can occur during installation.

[PreviousReference](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-widget/reference)
[NextBooking Engine API](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api)

Last updated 3 years ago

Was this helpful?

# Booking Engine Widget | Booking Engine Guide

The Booking Engine JavaScript Widget allows guests to book directly from the website of your property without being redirected elsewhere. It's a more advanced way of integrating the Mews Booking Engine into your website. This section describes how to use it.

*   [Availability blocks](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/use-cases/availability-blocks)

# Usage guidelines | Booking Engine Guide

This section provides guidelines and general information on how to use the **Mews Booking Engine API**. For information about individual endpoints or operations, see [API Operations](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/operations)
.

> **Important:** The Mews Booking Engine API is designed to be consumed directly by front-end clients. It is unsuitable for continuous polling by a single server due to its built-in anti-scraping protection and such requests can fail. For server to server communication, please refer to the [Mews Connector API](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/connector-api/)
> .

*   [Authentication](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/guidelines/authentication)
    
*   [Requests](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/guidelines/requests)
    
*   [Responses](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/guidelines/responses)
    
*   [Environments](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/guidelines/environments)
    
*   [Images](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/guidelines/images)
    
*   [Supported currency codes](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/guidelines/supported-currency-codes)
    
*   [Supported language codes](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/guidelines/supported-language-codes)
    

[PreviousBooking Engine API](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api)
[NextAuthentication](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/guidelines/authentication)

# API Operations | Booking Engine Guide

This section describes all operations supported by the API, organised by theme.

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/operations#availability)

Availability


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Operation or Endpoint

Description

[Get availability](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/operations/hotels#get-availability)

Get availability and pricing options for the specified hotel for the specified date interval

[Get availability blocks](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/operations/availability-blocks#get-availability-blocks)

Get details of the availability blocks for the given hotel.

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/operations#configuration)

Configuration


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Operation or Endpoint

Description

[Get configuration](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/operations/configuration#get-configuration)

Get configuration data for the specified booking engine instances; this operation can be called initially to fetch data which may be important during the booking workflow

[Get hotels](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/operations/hotels#get-hotels)

Get hotels data for a single specified hotel; this operation can be called initially to fetch data which may be important during the booking workflow

[Get payment configuration](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/operations/hotels#get-payment-configuration)

Fetch payment configuration parameters for the specified hotel

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/operations#payment-cards)

Payment cards


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Operation or Endpoint

Description

[Get payment cards](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/operations/payment-cards#get-payment-cards)

Fetch details about the listed payment cards, in particular the Authorization state

[Authorize payment card](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/operations/payment-cards#authorize-payment-card)

Request authorization of the specified payment card

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/operations#reservations)

Reservations


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Operation or Endpoint

Description

[Get reservations pricing](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/operations/reservations#get-reservations-pricing)

Get a price quotation for a specific hotel, date interval, room category and person count

[Get reservation price](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/operations/reservations#get-reservation-price)

Get final price of the specified reservations

[Create reservation group](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/operations/reservation-groups#create-reservation-group)

Create a group of one or more reservations, i.e. make a reservation

[Get reservation group](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/operations/reservation-groups#get-reservation-group)

Fetch details of the specified reservation group

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/operations#services)

Services


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Operation or Endpoint

Description

[Get services availability](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/operations/services#get-services-availability)

Get availability for the specified service for each time unit in the specified date interval

[Get services pricing](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/operations/services#get-services-pricing)

Get pricing for the specified service for each time unit in the specified date interval

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/operations#vouchers)

Vouchers


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Operation or Endpoint

Description

[Validate voucher](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/operations/vouchers#validate-voucher)

Determine if the specified voucher code is valid or not

[PreviousSupporting payment cards](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/use-cases/supporting-payment-cards)
[NextAvailability blocks](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/operations/availability-blocks)

# Mews Open API | Open API

Welcome to the **Mews Open API** developer documentation. Here you will find all the information you need to get started working with the **Mews Open API** as quickly as possible, as well as support in case you get stuck, and of course a full reference for each individual API. Let's jump in!

> #### 
> 
> [](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/open-api#partner-id)
> 
> Partner ID
> 
> You will be given a Partner ID at the start of your integration journey (e.g. INT123456), please keep this safe as you will need this when it's time to certify your integration. Not got one yet? [Register to join the Marketplace](https://www.mews.com/en/mews-marketplace-form)
> .

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/open-api#our-apis)

Our APIs


-------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [**Mews Connector API**](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/connector-api/)
     A general-purpose API that gives access to data and services in Mews, and supports multiple use cases.
    
*   [**Mews Channel Manager API**](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/channel-manager-api/)
     An API for Channel Managers and other distribution channels to fetch availability, rates and inventory data, and make reservations.
    
*   [**Mews Booking Engine API**](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/)
     An API for Booking Engines to enable your customers to create reservations directly in Mews.
    

Not sure which option is right for you? See [The Mews APIs](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/open-api/the-mews-apis)
. If you need further assistance, or have any questions or special requests, please contact [partnersuccess@mews.com](mailto:partnersuccess@mews.com)
.

> #### 
> 
> [](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/open-api#changes-to-the-documentation)
> 
> Changes to the documentation
> 
> To track changes and updates to this documentation, you can follow the [GitHub repository](https://github.com/MewsSystems/gitbook-open-api/tree/master)
> . For the individual APIs, we maintain Changelog and Deprecations pages, or you can also follow these on GitHub if you prefer - see [Staying up to date](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/open-api/staying-up-to-date)
> .

[NextGetting started](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/open-api/getting-started)

Last updated 2 years ago

Was this helpful?

# Getting started | Open API

The **Mews Open API** is a powerful tool that enables you to easily connect your hospitality software into Mews and become part of our ecosystem of integrated solutions. Use the **Mews Open API** to fetch data, make bookings, adjust rates, post charges, upsell products, and do a myriad of other things.

We take the 'open' part very seriously, which is why we make it as easy as possible to connect and why we are always trying to remove barriers to successful adoption. All the documentation is compact and straightforward and publicly hosted on [GitHub](https://github.com/MewsSystems)
, and we provide a Demo environment for developers so you can start coding and testing straight away.

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/open-api/getting-started#a-family-of-apis)

A family of APIs


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The **Mews Open API** is in fact a family of three APIs. Each API operates independently, serving a different function, and each has its own documentation.

*   See [The Mews APIs](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/open-api/the-mews-apis)
    

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/open-api/getting-started#what-do-you-want-to-achieve)

What do you want to achieve?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Take a look at [The Mews APIs](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/open-api/the-mews-apis)
 to see which is the API for you. The documentation for each API includes examples of common use cases for that API, or you can find an overview of all of them in [Use Cases](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/open-api/use-cases)
.

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/open-api/getting-started#getting-stuck-in)

Getting stuck in


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Each API includes a Guidelines section explaining how to use the API, including quick-start information for connecting to a Demo environment and getting results right away.

*   [Go straight to the Mews Connector API](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/connector-api/)
    
*   [Go straight to the Mews Channel Manager API](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/channel-manager-api/)
    
*   [Go straight to the Mews Booking Engine API](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/)
    

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/open-api/getting-started#help-with-terminology)

Help with terminology


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Throughout your Mews journey, you may find terms that are unfamiliar or unclear. That's why we created the [Mews Glossary for Open API users](https://help.mews.com/s/article/Mews-Glossary-for-Open-API-users?language=en_US)
. The Glossary provides a full description of all the terms used across the individual Mews APIs.

[PreviousMews Open API](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/open-api)
[NextMews Marketplace](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/open-api/mews-marketplace)

Last updated 3 years ago

Was this helpful?

# Mews Marketplace | Open API

The [Mews Marketplace](https://www.mews.com/en/products/marketplace)
 is where customers of Mews can find certified integration partners to help them improve operations, generate more revenue and enhance the guest experience. If you are a Mews partner, the Marketplace is the place to be!

> #### 
> 
> [](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/open-api/mews-marketplace#private-integrations)
> 
> Private integrations
> 
> Private integrations are where you make a private connection to a single enterprise or single property; in this case you would not be listed in the Marketplace.

[PreviousGetting started](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/open-api/getting-started)

# Booking Engine integrations | Open API

The steps for a Booking Engine API integration are as follows:

*   [Step 1: Explore the API](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/open-api/your-journey/booking-engine-integrations#step-1-exploration)
    
*   [Step 2: Register your client name](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/open-api/your-journey/booking-engine-integrations#step-2-registration)
    
*   [Step 3: Develop & test your solution](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/open-api/your-journey/booking-engine-integrations#step-3-development)
    
*   [Step 4: Go live in Production](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/open-api/your-journey/booking-engine-integrations#step-4-production)
    

If you have questions about the process, drop us a line to [partnersuccess@mews.com](mailto:partnersuccess@mews.com)
.

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/open-api/your-journey/booking-engine-integrations#step-1-exploration)

Step 1: Exploration


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Explore the [Booking Engine Guide](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/)
 and familiarize yourself with the API guidelines and operations. Not sure if the API is the right option? See [Booking Engine Guide ways to integrate](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/faq/ways-to-integrate)
.

> Please note that connection to the Booking Engine API is only available to Mews customers with Enterprise packages.

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/open-api/your-journey/booking-engine-integrations#step-2-registration)

Step 2: Registration


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Once you're sure you want to develop against the API, please register your client name and other details with Mews, as described in [Booking Engine API authorization](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/guidelines/authorization)
. To do so, send an email to [support@mews.com](mailto:support@mews.com)
 like the following example. In the meantime, you can start working with the API straight away using the sample client name, as described in [Booking Engine API authorization](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/guidelines/authorization)
.

> #### 
> 
> [](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/open-api/your-journey/booking-engine-integrations#registration-email)
> 
> Registration email
> 
> _Dear Mews support,_
> 
> _We would like to register the following client for Booking Engine access:_
> 
> *   _Client name:_ <insert your client name here>
>     
> *   _Contact email:_ <insert your contact email address here>
>     
> *   _Environments:_ <insert Demo and/or Production here>
>     

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/open-api/your-journey/booking-engine-integrations#step-3-development)

Step 3: Development


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can connect to our Demo environment to try out API operations, using your registered client name. Until your client name is registered, you can use the sample client name. All of the information you need to start developing and testing is in the [Booking Engine Guide](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/)
.

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/open-api/your-journey/booking-engine-integrations#step-4-production)

Step 4: Production


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Finally, when your development & testing is complete, you can switch over to the Production environment and you're all done, no certification needed! Note we support separate client name lists for the two environments, so make sure you are registered for the Production environment.

[PreviousYour journey with Mews](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/open-api/your-journey)
[NextStaying up to date](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/open-api/staying-up-to-date)

Last updated 3 years ago

Was this helpful?

# The Mews APIs | Open API

Mews currently supports three separate APIs, each serving a different purpose.

> #### 
> 
> [](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/open-api/the-mews-apis#three-individual-apis)
> 
> Three individual APIs
> 
> *   [Mews Connector API](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/open-api/the-mews-apis#mews-connector-api)
>     
> *   [Mews Channel Manager API](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/open-api/the-mews-apis#mews-channel-manager-api)
>     
> *   [Mews Booking Engine API](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/open-api/the-mews-apis#mews-booking-engine-api)
>     

The documentation for each API is self-contained and consists of two parts:

*   A set of guidelines on how to use the API
    
*   A detailed reference for all the API operations
    

And each API is hosted as a public GitHub repository.

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/open-api/the-mews-apis#mews-connector-api)

Mews Connector API


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This API is a general-purpose API that gives access to data and services in Mews Operations. The API supports many use cases, including Kiosk, Point Of Sale, Reservations Data, Upselling and Events Management, to name just a few. We encourage you to explore the API and innovate new solutions for our customers!

*   For the full documentation, see [Mews Connector API](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/connector-api/)
    

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/open-api/the-mews-apis#mews-channel-manager-api)

Mews Channel Manager API


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This API is for Channel Managers and other distribution channels to fetch availability, rates and inventory data, and make reservations.

*   For the full documentation, see [Mews Channel Manager API](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/channel-manager-api/)
    

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/open-api/the-mews-apis#mews-booking-engine-api)

Mews Booking Engine API


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This API is for booking engines to enable guests to create reservations directly in Mews. Please note that for custom booking engine solutions, connected properties will need a Mews Enterprise subscription.

*   For the full documentation, see [Mews Booking Engine API](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/)
    

> **Important:** The Mews Booking Engine API is designed to be consumed directly by front-end clients. It is unsuitable for continuous polling by a single server due to its built-in anti-scraping protection and such requests can fail. For server to server communication, please refer to the [Mews Connector API](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/connector-api/)
> .

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/open-api/the-mews-apis#which-api-to-use)

Which API to use?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you are a Channel Manager, or a bulk sales or distribution channel such as an Online Travel Agent, then you will want the [Mews Channel Manager API](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/channel-manager-api/)
. If you are implementing a Booking Engine for your customers to book with you directly, you will want the [Mews Booking Engine API](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/)
. For all other use cases, use the [Mews Connector API](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/connector-api/)
. Please also take a look at [Use Cases](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/open-api/use-cases)
, where you can find more information on individual use cases and links to more details in the documentation for the appropriate API.

[PreviousDeprecations Policy](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/open-api/staying-up-to-date/deprecations-policy)
[NextUse Cases](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/open-api/use-cases)

Last updated 3 years ago

Was this helpful?

# Jul 2022 Mewsletter | Open API

_26 Jul 2022_

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/open-api/staying-up-to-date/partner-newsletters/partner-mewsletter-jul22#api-versioning-share-your-thoughts)

API Versioning – Share your thoughts


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

TL;DR: We have a plan to add versioning to the Mews Connector API, but, first, we want to get your opinions. Click [here](https://mews.typeform.com/to/JCpBXN9h)
 to take a quick survey.

Now the full story:

We’ve come up with a strategy to speed up our development in a way that will provide you with higher performance endpoints, more rapidly roll out functionality for earlier adopters, and give all partners sufficient time to plan for upcoming, potentially high-impact changes.

What we’re talking about is adding versioning to the Mews Connector API. With the new approach, we would continue to make improvements that remain compatible with the current implementation, but if we need to make larger changes that cannot be made backwards compatible, we would then introduce a new version of the same endpoint that you have the choice to opt into.

Before we move ahead, though, **we want to get your thoughts on what would work best for your needs**. Of course, we’re also happy to talk further if you'd like.

[API Versioning Survey](https://mews.typeform.com/to/JCpBXN9h)

Your feedback is greatly appreciated.

~ The Mews Team

[PreviousOct 2022 Mewsletter](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/open-api/staying-up-to-date/partner-newsletters/partner-mewsletter-oct22)
[NextDeprecations Policy](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/open-api/staying-up-to-date/deprecations-policy)

# Getting started | Booking Engine Guide

The URL of the Booking Engine Standalone page has the following format:

Copy

    https://app.mews.com/distributor/aaaaaaaa-bbbb-cccc-dddd-eeeeeeeeeeee

The `aaaaaaaa-bbbb-cccc-dddd-eeeeeeeeeeee` part should be replaced with your Booking Engine Configuration ID. For details of how to obtain your Booking Engine Configuration ID, see the [FAQ](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/faq#where-can-i-get-configuration-id)
.

> Note:️ Make sure you are using Booking Engine Configuration ID, not Enterprise ID or some other ID.

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-standalone/getting-started#multi-enterprise)

Multi-enterprise


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you want to use a Booking Engine with multiple enterprises, you can place several Booking Engine Configurations IDs together, separated by a semicolon. Note in this case the _theme_ will be pulled from the ID of the first configuration in the URL.

Copy

    https://app.mews.com/distributor/aaaaaaaa-bbbb-cccc-dddd-eeeeeeeeeeee;ffffffff-gggg-hhhh-iiii-jjjjjjjjjjjj

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-standalone/getting-started#customization)

Customization


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can customize the behaviour of the the booking engine by using [Deeplinks](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-standalone/deeplinks)
.

[PreviousBooking Engine Standalone](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-standalone)
[NextDeeplinks](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-standalone/deeplinks)

# Google Tag Manager | Booking Engine Guide

> **Notice of usage:** Google Tag Manager (GTM) and Google Analytics 4 (GA4) are third party services and we provide this integration as is. We support a set of custom events and Data Layer variables for use with GTM and GA4, however we have no control over what happens to them and how they are used. The basic setup examples we provide have been tested and verified to work with the Mews Booking Engine, however if you need a more complex setup then we cannot provide the support to do so and we recommend to ask a specialist to set it up and test it for you.

> #### 
> 
> [](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/integrations/google-tag-manager#disclaimer-regarding-google-analytics-data-accuracy)
> 
> 🚨 Disclaimer regarding Google Analytics data accuracy
> 
> We understand that some property owners have expressed concerns about discrepancies between the data they see in Google Analytics (GA) and the actual reality. It’s essential to be aware of the following factors:
> 
> **Ad Blockers impact**
> 
> *   Approximately 33% of internet users utilize ad blockers, which can block Google Analytics and Google Tag Manager (GTM) scripts. See for example this article for a reference: [https://backlinko.com/ad-blockers-users](https://backlinko.com/ad-blockers-users)
>     .
>     
> *   Consequently, the data received from these services may not be 100% accurate.
>     
> *   Metrics such as revenue and the number of bookings may appear lower than the actual figures, due to ad-blocking behavior.
>     
> 
> **Consent and tracking**
> 
> *   If a guest declines cookies or tracking, their interactions won’t be tracked in Google Analytics.
>     
> 
> Please remember to address these considerations when interpreting GA data and making business decisions.

**Google Tag Manager (GTM)**, in conjunction with **Google Analytics 4 (GA4)**, is a supported integration with the **Mews Booking Engine Widget**. Both GTM and GA4 are part of the **Google Marketing Platform**, a suite of web marketing products and services.

*   [About Google Marketing Platform](https://marketingplatform.google.com/)
    
*   [About Google Tag Manager](https://marketingplatform.google.com/about/tag-manager/)
    
*   [About Google Analytics](https://marketingplatform.google.com/about/analytics/)
    

The Mews Booking Engine Widget includes code to support web marketing 'tags' that can be managed via Google Tag Manager, and which communicate data on user visits to Google Analytics for the purposes of web analytics. What this means is that with a Google Account you can access data on user visits, including page views and shopping cart behaviour.

> #### 
> 
> [](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/integrations/google-tag-manager#what-is-a-tag)
> 
> What is a Tag?
> 
> A Tag is something used to track activity on websites and apps, meaning the interaction between the user, their browser and the website or app. It's implemented as a piece of code inside the website or app that sends data to an analytics service (such as Google Analytics) when triggered to 'fire', usually by some event occurring within the website or app such as a page being requested by the user, or an item added to a shopping cart. As such, they provide invaluable information about how users are interacting with your digital property.

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/integrations/google-tag-manager#cross-domain-tracking)

Cross-domain tracking


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you use the **Mews Booking Engine Widget** on your website and collect data via **Google Analytics 4**, make sure you configure [cross-domain tracking](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/integrations/ga-cross-domain-tracking)
, to track users correctly across both your domain and the Mews domain.

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/integrations/google-tag-manager#ga4-vs-universal-analytics)

GA4 vs Universal Analytics


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The current version of Google Analytics is called Google Analytics 4 or GA4. This replaces the now obsolete Universal Analytics, which worked slightly differently and may have different terminology. Universal Analytics is being discontinued by Google and therefore we have removed all references to it in our documentation.

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/integrations/google-tag-manager#further-information)

Further information


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The whole subject of web marketing, web analytics and web marketing tags is rather complex and outside the scope of this documentation. However, you can find what you need to get started using it with Mews in the [Mews Help Center](https://help.mews.com/)
. Google also provides online support resources.

### 

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/integrations/google-tag-manager#mews-support)

Mews Support

*   [Set up Google Tag Manager](https://help.mews.com/s/article/google-tag-manager)
    
*   [All GTM related articles](https://help.mews.com/s/global-search/GTM)
    

### 

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/integrations/google-tag-manager#google-support)

Google Support

*   [Google Tag Manager Help](https://support.google.com/tagmanager/)
    
*   [Google Analytics Help](https://support.google.com/analytics/)
    

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/integrations/google-tag-manager#getting-started)

Getting started


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Here we provide the reference information you will need, so if you are already familiar with Google Tag Manager you can get started straight away. The reference includes details of **custom events** and **Data Layer variables** generated within the Booking Engine, which can be used to trigger analytics tags to fire, i.e. to send data to Google Analytics. You will need to reference these events and variables when setting up tag _triggers_ in Google Tag Manager.

*   [Google Triggers Reference](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/integrations/google-triggers-reference)
    

[PreviousIntegrations](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/integrations)
[NextGoogle Triggers Reference](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/integrations/google-triggers-reference)

# Ways to integrate | Booking Engine Guide

You can integrate with the **Mews Booking Engine** in one of three ways. Which one should you choose?

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/faq/ways-to-integrate#booking-engine-standalone)

Booking Engine Standalone


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you’re not sure which integration method to use, go with the standalone option. It’s the simplest way to connect your website with the Mews Booking Engine and enable your guests to make direct bookings. We will provide you with a link to a page where your Booking Engine instance is located. For more information, see [Booking Engine Standalone](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-standalone)
 or open a ticket from Mews Operations via our Mews Digital Assistant.

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/faq/ways-to-integrate#booking-engine-widget)

Booking Engine Widget


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you're a developer, you might be interested in a more advanced way to integrate the Mews Booking Engine into your website. For a more seamless experience, the Booking Engine JavaScript Widget allows guests to book directly from the website of your property without being redirected elsewhere. For more information, see [Booking Engine Widget](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-widget)
.

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/faq/ways-to-integrate#booking-engine-api)

Booking Engine API


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you would like to implement your own custom booking engine that connects directly with **Mews Operations**, have a look at the [Booking Engine API](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api)
. Note that this option is only available to customers with an Enterprise subscription. Should you be on a different subscription and are interested in this option, please contact [customersuccess@mews.com](mailto:customersuccess@mews.com)
.

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/faq/ways-to-integrate#need-help)

Need help?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Browse the Guide to see if your question is answered, but if not and you need further assistance, you can open a ticket from Mews Operations via our Mews Digital Assistant.

[PreviousFAQ](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/faq)
[NextMigration off the mews.li domain](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/faq/mews-li-migration)

# Authentication | Booking Engine Guide

The **Mews Booking Engine API** is a public API that requires client authentication and authorization.

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/guidelines/authentication#client-authentication)

Client authentication


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Authentication is the process of verifying the identity of the client. To access the API, you must identify your client application by providing the `Client` property in all requests. This ensures that your client application is recognized and allowed to interact with the API.

### 

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/guidelines/authentication#registration)

Registration

Your client application needs to be pre-registered with Mews Support. You can open a ticket from **Mews Operations** via the [Mews Digital Assistant](https://help.mews.com/s/article/How-to-use-the-Mews-Digital-Assistant)
. The registration request should contain:

*   `Client` - the name of the client application that will be used for every API request
    
*   `Email` - an email contact for your development department; this email will be used by our developers to notify you about any breaking changes in the API
    
*   `Environment` - the name of the environment you are accessing, either `Production` or `Demo`.
    

### 

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/guidelines/authentication#environments)

Environments

We offer two environments, `Production` and `Demo`. Use `Demo` during API implementation, and `Production` only for live customer sites. The two environments have separate client lists, so make sure you are registered in `Production` before you move your implementation to the Production environment. For details, see our [Environments](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/guidelines/environments)
 page.

### 

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/guidelines/authentication#sample-client-name)

Sample client name

Before the registration of your `Client` name is confirmed, you can use the sample client name below. This client name will **only work in the Demo environment**. Keep in mind that this must be replaced by your proper `Client` name as soon as you finish the registration process.

Copy

    {
        "Client": "My Client 1.0.0"
    }

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/guidelines/authentication#client-authorization)

Client authorization


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Authorization is the process of determining what the authenticated client is allowed to do. In this case, it is sufficient to know the unique identifier of a hotel or other enterprise in order to access it. However, the client must be authenticated by providing the `Client` property in all requests to ensure it has the necessary permissions to interact with the API.

[PreviousUsage guidelines](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/guidelines)
[NextRequests](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/guidelines/requests)

# Availability blocks | Booking Engine Guide

Availability blocks are fixed sets of inventory set aside from public availability for private groups such as wedding parties, travel agencies or corporate clients. If you have access to these private blocks, you can use them in the API. To use an availability block, you will need to obtain its `availabilityBlockId`.

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/use-cases/availability-blocks#how-to-obtain-availability-block-id)

How to obtain availability block ID


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can obtain a unique availability block ID from the Availability Blocks screen in **Mews Operations**, under 'Booking engine link'. Multiple IDs can be created, in case you have multiple booking engine instances.

> Note: This functionality requires the property to have an _Enterprise subscription_.

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/use-cases/availability-blocks#how-to-work-with-availability-blocks)

How to work with availability blocks


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Use [Get availability blocks](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/operations/availability-blocks#get-availability-blocks)
 to fetch details about your availability block. Check that the current date is between `StartUtc` and `EndUtc` to see if the availability block is valid, or the block has expired. Then you can supply `availabilityBlockId` into all the API operations that accept it (see below). To get the appropriate rate, filter [Rates](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/operations/hotels#rate)
 with the `rateId` from the fetched availability block details. Only this rate should be available and bookable for this booking engine session.

### 

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/use-cases/availability-blocks#endpoints-accepting-availability-block-id)

Endpoints accepting availability block ID

*   [Get availability](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/operations/hotels#get-availability)
    
*   [Get reservations pricing](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/operations/reservations#get-reservations-pricing)
    
*   [Create reservation group](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/operations/reservation-groups#create-reservation-group)
    

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/use-cases/availability-blocks#further-information)

Further information


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For more information about availability blocks, the following guide may be helpful. You can also use the Search function to find other suitable content in the Mews Help system.

*   [Creating availability blocks](https://help.mews.com/s/article/Creating-availability-blocks-in-Mews?language=en_US)
    

[PreviousUse cases](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/use-cases)
[NextOn session payments](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/use-cases/on-session-payments)

# Deeplinks | Booking Engine Guide

With deeplinks you can create URLs which open Booking Engine Standalone in some pre-defined setup, for example with a specific currency or specific dates. You do this by simply adding [supported parameters](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-standalone/deeplinks#supported-parameters)
 to the URL in the form of a URL query string. For example:

Copy

    https://app.mews.com/distributor/aaaaaaaa-bbbb-cccc-dddd-eeeeeeeeeeee?currency=EUR&mewsRoute=rates&mewsRoom=aaaaaaaa-bbbb-cccc-dddd-eeeeeeeeeeee

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-standalone/deeplinks#supported-parameters)

Supported parameters


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This is the list of parameters that can be added to the URL query string. Parameters can be combined, and some parameters have no effect unless they are used in combination, e.g. `mewsHotel`.

### 

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-standalone/deeplinks#parameters-supported-in-single-and-multi-enterprise-mode)

Parameters supported in single and multi-enterprise mode

Name

Description

Example

mewsStart

an arrival date in ISO 8601 format (`YYYY-MM-DD`)

`2023-01-20` for January 20, 2023

mewsEnd

a departure date in ISO 8601 format (`YYYY-MM-DD`)

`2023-01-23` for January 23, 2023

mewsVoucherCode

a voucher code

`E1A71167851A30043B12`

mewsRoute

[mewsRoute](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-standalone/deeplinks#mewsroute)

`rooms` for rooms step

mewsSort

sort categories on category step by lowest/highest price; overrides all other ordering methods

`mewsSort=asc` sorts by lowest price, `mewsSort=desc` sorts by highest price

mewsRoom

opens with specified room selected (`aaaaaaaa-bbbb-cccc-dddd-eeeeeeeeeeee`)

`da394bbb-9685-4bb8-9547-ab7300915967`

mewsAdultCount

number of adults that should be selected by default

`3`

mewsChildCount

number of children that should be selected by default

`1`

language

a language code (`xx-YY`)

`en-US` for U.S. English

currency

a currency code (`XXX`)

`USD` for United States dollar

### 

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-standalone/deeplinks#additional-parameters-supported-in-multi-enterprise-mode)

Additional parameters supported in multi-enterprise mode

In addition, Mews Booking Engine in multi-enterprise mode also supports:

Name

Description

Example

mewsCityId

selects specified city (`aaaaaaaa-bbbb-cccc-dddd-eeeeeeeeeeee`)

`cf1678c0-0896-450b-8611-bec07d63cc32`

mewsHotel

selects specified hotel (`aaaaaaaa-bbbb-cccc-dddd-eeeeeeeeeeee`)

`e31209f1-8be9-49d0-a577-ab73009151f3`

### 

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-standalone/deeplinks#mewsroute)

mewsRoute

With parameter `mewsRoute` you can open the Mews Booking Engine on a specific step, e.g. selecting a room (or other bookable space) or selecting a rate.

> Note: The steps available depend on whether you are using single-enterprise or multi-enterprise mode. Some steps also require additional parameters to be set, otherwise the mewsRoute parameter will not work correctly (see the following tables for details).

#### 

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-standalone/deeplinks#mewsroute-in-single-enterprise-mode)

mewsRoute in single-enterprise mode

Step

Required parameters

What it does

`mewsRoute=rooms`

none

Application will open a page where user can select a room category.

`mewsRoute=rates`

mewsRoom

Application will open a page where user can select rate, products and occupancy.

#### 

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-standalone/deeplinks#mewsroute-in-multi-enterprise-mode)

mewsRoute in multi-enterprise mode

Step

Required parameters

What it does

`mewsRoute=hotels`

mewsCityId

Application will open a page where user can select a hotel (or other property type).

`mewsRoute=rooms`

mewsCityId, mewsHotel

Application will open a page where user can select a room category (or other space type category).

`mewsRoute=rates`

mewsCityId, mewsHotel, mewsRoom

Application will open a page where user can select rate, products and occupancy.

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-standalone/deeplinks#examples)

Examples


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-standalone/deeplinks#example-1-specific-start-date-voucher-code-and-language)

Example 1: Specific start date, voucher code and language

The following deeplink will open the booking engine with a specific start date, specific voucher code and specific language:

Copy

    https://app.mews.com/distributor/aaaaaaaa-bbbb-cccc-dddd-eeeeeeeeeeee?mewsStart=2021-01-01&mewsVoucherCode=special-discount&language=en-US

### 

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-standalone/deeplinks#example-2-pre-selected-room-and-currency-on-rate-selection-step)

Example 2: Pre-selected room and currency on rate selection step

The following deeplink will open the booking engine on the rate selection step with a specific pre-selected room and specific currency:

Copy

    https://app.mews.com/distributor/aaaaaaaa-bbbb-cccc-dddd-eeeeeeeeeeee?currency=EUR&mewsRoute=rates&mewsRoom=aaaa-bbbb-cccc-dddd

### 

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-standalone/deeplinks#example-3-multi-enterprise-with-pre-selected-city-on-hotel-selection-step)

Example 3: Multi-enterprise with pre-selected city on hotel selection step

The following deeplink will open the booking engine in multi-enterprise mode on the hotel selection step with a specific pre-selected city:

Copy

    https://app.mews.com/distributor/aaaaaaaa-bbbb-cccc-dddd-eeeeeeeeeeee;ffffffff-gggg-hhhh-iiii-jjjjjjjjjjjj?mewsRoute=hotels&mewsCityId=aaaa-bbbb-cccc-dddd

# Availability blocks | Booking Engine Guide

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/operations/availability-blocks#get-availability-blocks)

Get availability blocks


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Get details of the availability blocks for the given hotel. This operation can be called initially to fetch data which may be important during the booking workflow. Availability blocks can restrict your booking engine's calendar to specific intervals defined by `StartUtc` and `EndUtc` in the response, it also gives you `RateId` that should be used.

### 

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/operations/availability-blocks#request)

Request

`[ApiBaseUrl]/api/distributor/v1/availabilityBlocks/getAll`

Copy

    {
        "Client": "My Client 1.0.0",
        "AvailabilityBlockIds": [\
            "5mgbe1b4-6739-40b7-81b3-d369d9469c48"\
        ],
        "EnterpriseId": "3edbe1b4-6739-40b7-81b3-d369d9469c48"
    }

Property

Type

Contract

Description

`Client`

string

required

Identification of the API client, as described in [Authentication](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/guidelines/authentication)
.

`EnterpriseId`

string

required

Unique identifier of the hotel (enterprise).

`AvailabilityBlockIds`

array of string

required

Set of unique identifiers of the Availability Blocks for which you want to get the details.

### 

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/operations/availability-blocks#response)

Response

Copy

    {
        "AvailabilityBlocks":[\
          {\
            "Id": "5mgbe1b4-6739-40b7-81b3-d369d9469c48",\
            "Name": "Name of the availability block",\
            "ServiceId": "a64f85bf-b92c-4df7-b7c8-ab7c00adc59a",\
            "RateId": "038a88e6-17c6-4553-b036-aebb00a9bc4c",\
            "StartUtc": "2022-06-27T22:00:00Z",\
            "EndUtc": "2022-07-04T22:00:00Z"\
          }\
        ]
    }

Property

Type

Contract

Description

`Id`

string

required

Provided ID of availability block.

`Name`

string

required

Name of availability block.

`ServiceId`

string

required

Unique identifier of [Service](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/operations/configuration#service)
 to which availability block is assigned

`RateId`

string

required

Unique identifier of [Rate](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/operations/hotels#rate)
 which is intended for this availability block

`StartUtc`

string

required

Availability block start date (validity start date) in ISO 8601 format.

`EndUtc`

string

required

Availability block end date (validity expiration date) in ISO 8601 format.

[PreviousAPI Operations](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/operations)
[NextConfiguration](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/operations/configuration)

Last updated 9 months ago

Was this helpful?

# Migration off the mews.li domain | Booking Engine Guide

This is a guide to help you migrate your booking engine off the discontinued `mews.li` domain.

> **Important:** Support for the old domain was discontinued in May 2024 - we are not responsible for the functionality of the booking engine on this domain.

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/faq/mews-li-migration#standalone-booking-engine-migration)

Standalone Booking Engine migration


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Find every occurrence of links containing `https://mews.li` domain pointing to the standalone booking engine hosted on our domain and replace them with `https://app.mews.com`. See [Standalone implementation guide](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-standalone/getting-started)
.

### 

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/faq/mews-li-migration#example)

Example

#### 

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/faq/mews-li-migration#deprecated-implementation)

❌ Deprecated implementation

Copy

    <a href="https://www.mews.li/distributor/6b87e134-8c75-468a-82d4-aca900c43c70">Book Now</a>

#### 

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/faq/mews-li-migration#after-migration-implementation)

✅ After migration implementation

Copy

    <a href="https://app.mews.com/distributor/6b87e134-8c75-468a-82d4-aca900c43c70">Book Now</a>

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/faq/mews-li-migration#widget-booking-engine-migration)

Widget Booking Engine migration


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Replace the domain in your booking engine loading script from `https://mews.li` to `https://api.mews.com`. See [installation guideline](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-widget/getting-started)
.

#### 

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/faq/mews-li-migration#deprecated-implementation-1)

❌ Deprecated implementation

Copy

    <head>
        ...
        <script src="https://mews.li/distributor/distributor.min.js"></script>
        ...
    </head>

#### 

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/faq/mews-li-migration#after-migration-implementation-1)

✅ After migration implementation

Copy

    <head>
        ...
        <script src="https://api.mews.com/distributor/distributor.min.js"></script>
        ...
    </head>

After a successful migration, the keyword `mews.li` should no longer appear on your website.

If you have any questions, please open a ticket from **Mews Operations** via the Mews Digital Assistant.

[PreviousWays to integrate](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/faq/ways-to-integrate)
[NextChangelog](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/changelog)

Last updated 9 months ago

Was this helpful?

# Google Tag Manager Configuration | Booking Engine Guide

This guide provides a streamlined process for exporting and configuring a Google Tag Manager (GTM) skeleton suitable for booking engine. Follow these precise steps to efficiently adapt your GTM setup to new requirements.

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/integrations/gtm-skeleton#prepare-your-configuration)

Prepare your configuration


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Download the configuration file:**
    
    *   Access the prepared skeleton configuration file: [Google Tag Manager - Configuration.json](https://github.com/MewsSystems/gitbook-booking-engine/blob/master/.gitbook/assets/GTM-Mews.json)
        .
        
    
2.  **IMPORTANT: Customize the configuration:**
    
    *   Open the downloaded JSON file in your preferred text editor.
        
    *   Replace all occurrences of `_GA4_ID_` with your actual Google Analytics 4 (GA4) tracking ID.
        
    
3.  **Prepare for import:**
    
    *   Save the changes to the JSON file, ensuring it is ready to be imported into your GTM account.
        
    

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/integrations/gtm-skeleton#import-configuration-into-google-tag-manager)

Import configuration into Google Tag Manager


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/integrations/gtm-skeleton#import-the-modified-file)

Import the modified file:

*   **Navigate to import options:**
    
    *   In your GTM account, go to the **Admin** tab.
        
    *   Under the container options, select **Import Container**.
        
    
*   **Select and upload file:**
    
    *   Click on **Choose file** and select your modified JSON file.
        
    *   Decide how to merge this configuration with any existing setup. Options include:
        
        *   **Overwrite**: Replaces the current container with the imported one.
            
        *   **Merge**: Combines the imported configuration with the existing one, with options to resolve conflicts.
            
        *   **Rename**: Adds the imported configuration while renaming any conflicts.
            
        
    
*   **Complete the import:**
    
    *   Follow prompts to finalize the import process.
        
    

### 

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/integrations/gtm-skeleton#update-and-publish)

Update and publish:

*   **Review configuration:**
    
    *   Thoroughly check all tags, triggers, and variables to ensure they are correctly configured.
        
    
*   **Test before publishing:**
    
    *   Utilize GTM's preview mode to test the setup. Ensure that all configurations perform as expected.
        
    
*   **Publish changes:**
    
    *   Once verified, publish the container to apply your configurations live.
        
    

[PreviousGoogle Triggers Reference](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/integrations/google-triggers-reference)
[NextGoogle Analytics cross-domain tracking](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/integrations/ga-cross-domain-tracking)

Last updated 9 months ago

Was this helpful?

# On session payments | Booking Engine Guide

Whenever a user creates a reservation, there is an option to allow them to pay directly. This needs to be correctly configured via settlement rules on `RateGroup`. We provide this functionality only for `Rates` where the payment card is charged automatically at the time of creating the reservation. In order to simplify the whole payment processing workflow we offer this functionality in our applications via a feature called "Payment request".

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/use-cases/on-session-payments#creating-a-reservation-group)

Creating a reservation group


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The first step of the entire workflow is to create a reservation group via the API, using [Create reservation group](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/operations/reservation-groups#create-reservation-group)
. The response contains a field `PaymentRequestId` which we will use for a redirect to an application that can handle the payment. The payment gateway supports an optional query parameter `returnUrl` which will be used to return the user into your booking engine after successful payment or in case the user decides to abandon the flow. The `returnUrl` value should be a Base64-encoded absolute URL, e.g. in JavaScript via the `btoa` function. After the user returns to your booking engine, you can verify the state of the payment request by calling [Get reservation group](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/operations/reservation-groups#get-reservation-group)
 with `Extent` for `PaymentRequests` and optionally for `Payments` which you want to validate. Validation should be done mainly on the [Payment request state](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/operations/reservation-groups#payment-request-state)
 and optionally [Payment state](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/operations/reservation-groups#payment-state)
.

[](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/use-cases/on-session-payments#step-by-step-workflow)

Step by step workflow


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  [Create reservation group](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/operations/reservation-groups#create-reservation-group)
    .
    
2.  Get `PaymentRequestId` from the response.
    
3.  Create a `ReturnUrl`, encoding your URL with `Base64` e.g. JavaScript example would be `btoa(urlWhereUserShouldReturn)`.
    
4.  Redirect the user to the gateway with URL `https://[MewsApplicationsBaseUrl]/navigator/payment-requests/detail/[PaymentRequestId]?returnUrl=[ReturnUrl]` (you can find the value of `MewsApplicationBaseUrl` in the [Environments](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/guidelines/environments)
     section).
    
5.  After the user returns to the `ReturnUrl` in your booking engine you can verify the state by using [Get reservation group](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/operations/reservation-groups#get-reservation-group)
     with a specified [Reservation group extent](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/operations/reservation-groups#reservation-group-extent)
    .
    
6.  Validate the state of the Payment request in the response.
    

> **Note:** Until the Payment request enters its finite state (see [Payment request state](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/operations/reservation-groups#payment-request-state)
> ) you can re-direct the user again, for example with a "Try to pay again" button.

[PreviousAvailability blocks](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/use-cases/availability-blocks)
[NextPayment card authorization](https://mews-systems.gitbook.io/booking-engine-guide/booking-engine-api/use-cases/payment-card-authorization)

Last updated 3 years ago
